Ordered two large family size dry pot to share for a company luncheon of 7 ppl. Good variety of vegetables found in both dishes. There's a great amount of flavor in both of the dishes. It comes with individual rice and the seafood even has vermicelli noodles at the bottom. Next time I would like to try their fish dry pot.< /review>

< Review>
Very nice dry pots - meat and vegetables without a soup base served in a wok-like pan over flame. We also had a chao mian/chow mein which was richly flavored and excellent as well.

The downside - we went about 25 minutes before closing and the waitress twitched impatiently at the table waiting for us to order. Don't go near closing time.</Review>

The grilled live fish in Figure 3 must have a point, $39 (live fish/fresh fish), and have eaten a few live fish in the past year (the boss said it is a live fish), but after a taste, you will know that it is not, but today This is really a live fish, the bite is different.

<Rate>4</Rate><Text>This resembles more of a house party rather than "club". I decided to hit up the CA club scene and see the difference between NY/LA. Firstly, the club opens at 9pm and closes at about 2am. When I first walked in, it was still pretty empty so I headed to the bar to order drinks. It was $13 for a mixed drink and $10 for a beer, talk about inflation. Good thing the amaretto sour I ordered was pretty strong and I was soon partying the night away! Note: However, I also wanted a Jager bomb; but they do not make those. I came to APT503 on a Saturday night, and apparently it was 'R&B Night' so I was sad there was no ratchet music for me to dance to. Nevertheless, I had a lot of fun taking pictures with the decor as well as dancing in front of the DJ booth. If you're looking for a trendy place to take IG pics and enjoy music with friends, come to Apt. 503. Oh and this place tends to cater to the younger crowd, I noticed multiple groups of people who "just turned 21".</Text>< Pics>

Location is clean, and compared to the other gyms I've been to (Planet Fitness, LA Fitness and 24 Hour Fitness), it's a lot less crowded, even during peak hours. I think the attached UFC Gym scares people away thinking Crunch is a specialized or MMA gym.

My only complaint would be the hours and contracts, but those are both pretty standard for most modern gyms, the pricing is super fair, just wait for a special signup event.< /review><pics>None</pics>< resp>

< text>
This is a really comfortable neighborhood spot for burgers, drinks, and the occasional sporting event. It's not really a sports bar, but they'll break out some extra screens for big games.

There is great outdoor seating as well as a small library of board games.

The burgers are great, and they have a decent beer selection. The only real problem is that the service is slow. It only gets worse when it's packed for the Warriors games. If you're not in a rush, though, this place is great.< /text>

nick papcun< /Name>
< text>
It should be telling when you roll up at prime lunch time on a gorgeous sunday and a beer garden why outdoor seating is empty.

When your beer garden has 14 taps of 'local beer' and 8 of those taps are IPA's, that's a horrible selection.  When your local beer list contains Sierra Nevada, Bear Republic, Drakes and Golden State, all redily available at a Safeway, that's a horrible selection.

If you have the beer love of an aging dad-bro and are into saving money and never waiting instead of good service (holy hell it's slow, took us 15 minutes to get our beers when the place was empty except for 3 small 2 tops/3 tops) this is the place for you.  Bring your dad when he comes from out of town and you need someplace no one you know will recognize you when he's spouting midwest rants about Crazy Cali and sjws.  This place is perfect.< /text>

< review>
Came across this place during grocery shopping and I was pleasantly surprised.  The interior felt like a restaurant and not your regular fast food place.  Table and seats were high and there were also regular seating too.  After I ordered, I was given a number, which I took to my table.  I really liked seeing the sink by the counter, where I could just wash my hands before eating.  My burger was delivered to my table and all the condiments and napkins were at the table too. None of those little packets and napkin dispensers at the counter to mess about.  The burger was tasty and looked freshly made and all the onions and tomatoes freshly cut.  Worth a visit for a quick bite and friendly staff that keep the place clean and inviting.

I had eaten somewhat recently and wasnt overly hungry so I opted for just the single patty burger with no fries or drink but with all the toppings it was as big as a double or triple anyway and satisfying. The angus burger on special was topped with beef brisket, bacon, cheddar, and pickles and the huge stack of juicy, crisp, cheese covered meat was delicious. The pickles went well with the other salty flavors and the hearty bun had no issues handling the mountain of greasy meats. I didnt notice any of the bbq sauce I was expecting on it but they threw in a few packs of ketchup which I didnt use and it was great dry regardless.

Staff were friendly and service quick and efficient. They took every corona safety precaution I could think of with sanitizers, social distancing markers, and staff decked out in protective gear. No outdoor dining area and just carryout and delivery orders currently tho.</review>

This place is in the same class as Burger Joint and Super Duper.  A premium priced fast food of better quality.  The burgers range from 6-7$ alone, with small sides of fries for around $2.
I ordered a truffle swiss chicken sandwich with smash fries (super thin fries tossed in garlic, rosemary, olive oil).  The fries were a bit over oily and salty, but were crispy and tasty.  The thinness made them not ideal vehicles for ketchup.  The sandwich looked thrown together with the bun not even covering most of the chicken, and they forgot to put veggies in it I had to bring it back.  It was also really greasy but tasted good.  I ended up with a strange stomach ache so I walked around Ross in the plaza which is extremely depressing.  Not likely to repeat here without coupon.<//text>

<UserId.>104032290699854711173</UserId.><username>Erik Toth< /username><date>1528567309908</date><Rating>1< /Rating>< review>
This was my second visit to this location. Both were bad experiences. After waiting for 25 minutes, I never actually got my burger. They put all of their focus on DoorDash orders at the sacrifice of all sit-down customers (about 10 people). You place an order at the counter and then sit at a table with your order number. 5 out of the 10 people waiting at tables had their order "lost".

This place wants to have a gimmick and be something like Five Guys but it can't even compete with a quality burger from Jack-In-The-Box.

Both times, my order was taken by a careless staff member. I was never explained what the "smash" process was and was not asked for a temp on my meat. (For my first visit) what I got was an expensive and very mediocre greasy thin burger on what seems like a store bought bun. Not worth it.

Atmosphere is a step up from fast food environment. Save your money for a Five Guys Burger or Jack-In-The-Box. Both deliver better products and experience.</review>

<Gmap_id>0x808f7e2fcae1b335:0xe188bf359e46ad52<//Gmap_id><Resp>None< /Resp><Name>Johnny Wang< /Name>< review>
I came here for an event a few weeks back, and basically got to try, well, every single one of the items on their menu, so I'm not going to go and rate each individual one. But, overall, everything they have to offer is pretty solid, from their various burgers, to their sides, to their shakes (which are made with Haagen Daz ice cream!). Fantastic, they are not, but solid, they are, falling somewhere in between the fast food world and the fancy burger world, in the same tier as, say, Super Duper.

Some interesting tidbits: they're named what they are because they take fresh meat (ground beef, chicken, etc) and smash it into a super hot griddle, which simultaneously sears, steams, and quickly cooks the meat. Also, while they have set items on their menus, their burgers are actually customizable, for those who like playing with their food. And with the variety of buns, proteins, and ingredients to pick from, there's plenty of combinations to come up with!

***Accessibility Info***

Venue - Spacious venue, with a combination of inaccessible counter height tables, and lower standard height tables and booths.

Bathroom - Didn't check them out, but I imagine they're okay.</review>
